<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="what-claude-code-does-for-you"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#what-claude-code-does-for-you" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">â€‹<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">What Claude Code does for you</span></h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Build features from descriptions</strong>: Tell Claude what you want to build in plain English. It will make a plan, write the code, and ensure it works.</li>
<li><strong>Debug and fix issues</strong>: Describe a bug or paste an error message. Claude Code will analyze your codebase, identify the problem, and implement a fix.</li>
<li><strong>Navigate any codebase</strong>: Ask anything about your teamâ€™s codebase, and get a thoughtful answer back. Claude Code maintains awareness of your entire project structure, can find up-to-date information from the web, and with <a class="link" href="/docs/en/mcp">MCP</a> can pull from external data sources like Google Drive, Figma, and Slack.</li>
<li><strong>Automate tedious tasks</strong>: Fix fiddly lint issues, resolve merge conflicts, and write release notes. Do all this in a single command from your developer machines, or automatically in CI.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="why-developers-love-claude-code"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#why-developers-love-claude-code" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">â€‹<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Why developers love Claude Code</span></h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Works in your terminal</strong>: Not another chat window. Not another IDE. Claude Code meets you where you already work, with the tools you already love.</li>
<li><strong>Takes action</strong>: Claude Code can directly edit files, run commands, and create commits. Need more? <a class="link" href="/docs/en/mcp">MCP</a> lets Claude read your design docs in Google Drive, update your tickets in Jira, or use <em>your</em> custom developer tooling.</li>
<li><strong>Unix philosophy</strong>: Claude Code is composable and scriptable. <code>tail -f app.log | claude -p &quot;Slack me if you see any anomalies appear in this log stream&quot;</code> <em>works</em>. Your CI can run <code>claude -p &quot;If there are new text strings, translate them into French and raise a PR for @lang-fr-team to review&quot;</code>.</li>
<li><strong>Enterprise-ready</strong>: Use the Claude API, or host on AWS or GCP. Enterprise-grade <a class="link" href="/docs/en/security">security</a>, <a class="link" href="/docs/en/data-usage">privacy</a>, and <a href="https://trust.anthropic.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">compliance</a> is built-in.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="use-claude-code-everywhere"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#use-claude-code-everywhere" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">â€‹<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Use Claude Code everywhere</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Claude Code works across your development environment: in your terminal, in your IDE, in the cloud, and in Slack.</span>
<ul>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/quickstart">Terminal (CLI)</a></strong>: the core Claude Code experience. Run <code>claude</code> in any terminal to start coding.</li>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/claude-code-on-the-web">Claude Code on the web</a></strong>: use Claude Code from your browser at <a href="https://claude.ai/code" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">claude.ai/code</a> or the Claude iOS app, with no local setup required. Run tasks in parallel, work on repos you donâ€™t have locally, and review changes in a built-in diff view.</li>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/desktop">Desktop app</a></strong>: a standalone application with diff review, parallel sessions via git worktrees, and the ability to launch cloud sessions.</li>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/vs-code">VS Code</a></strong>: a native extension with inline diffs, @-mentions, and plan review.</li>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/jetbrains">JetBrains IDEs</a></strong>: a plugin for IntelliJ IDEA, PyCharm, WebStorm, and other JetBrains IDEs with IDE diff viewing and context sharing.</li>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/github-actions">GitHub Actions</a></strong>: automate code review, issue triage, and other workflows in CI/CD with <code>@claude</code> mentions.</li>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/gitlab-ci-cd">GitLab CI/CD</a></strong>: event-driven automation for GitLab merge requests and issues.</li>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/slack">Slack</a></strong>: mention Claude in Slack to route coding tasks to Claude Code on the web and get PRs back.</li>
<li><strong><a class="link" href="/docs/en/chrome">Chrome</a></strong>: connect Claude Code to your browser for live debugging, design verification, and web app testing.</li>
</ul>
